## Sustainability features

Organic content

Product contains at least 95% organic material.

As certified by

USDA Organic

## USDA Organic

* * *

USDA Organic certified products are required to be produced using farming practices that maintain and improve soil and water quality, reduce the use of synthetic materials, conserve biodiversity, and avoid genetic engineering, among other factors. Crops can be certified organic if they're grown without prohibited substances such as most synthetic fertilizers and pesticides for three years prior to harvest. Livestock are raised on pastures and treated humanely without growth hormones or antibiotics. Organic products do not contain GMOs or artificial colors, flavors, or preservatives. USDA Organic products contain a minimum of 95% organic ingredients and use the USDA Organic seal.

[Learn more about this certification](https://www.ams.usda.gov/services/organic-certification/organic-basics)

# About this item

- Terrasoul Superfoods Organic Pea Protein Powder (80% Protein), 1.5 Pounds
- USDA Certified Organic, Non-GMO, Gluten-Free, Vegan
- Our protein powder isoltate is made from USDA certified organic yellow peas and laboratory tested for purity
- Having a minimal flavor our pea protein is perfect for post workout recovery and adding protein to recipes

## Product Description

About Terrasoul Superfoods Organic Pea Protein:

Pea protein is a unique source of plant based protein that is rich in amino acids, works effectively at preventing muscle wear and tear, and digests easily.

Its silky smooth texture and mild flavor make it the perfect addition to any smoothie, or added in combination with other protein powders.

Our pea protein contains no “natural” flavors or fillers. We use only the most pure and thoughtfully sourced plant based ingredients and laboratory test each batch for purity.

Potential Health Benefits of Pea Protein:

~ Pea protein has a great amino acid profile, including a lot of the branched-chain amino acids that are well-known for decreasing muscle breakdown after workouts.

~ Pea protein can aid in weight loss since a great feature of pea protein is its ability to lower levels of the hunger hormone, ghrelin.

Suggested Uses: Having a minimal flavor our pea protein is perfect for post workout recovery and adding concentrated plant powered protein to recipes.

About Terrasoul Superfoods:

Our mission at Terrasoul Superfoods is to distribute the freshest, most nutrient-dense foods grown with integrity in healthy soils on sustainable, organic farms.

Working in close partnership with our suppliers enables us to offer the highest quality ingredients at a superior value.

Find us on Instagram and Facebook for tips on how to use our ingredients and superfood recipes.

### Product Safety and Compliance DetailsProduct Safety and Compliance Details

### Safe use

As the [Food and Drug Administration (FDA)](https://www.fda.gov/media/158337/download?attachment) advises, dietary supplements can support your overall health but may also have powerful effects on the body. It’s important to read labels carefully, exercise caution, and consult your healthcare professional before taking any supplement. Side effects are more likely if supplements are taken in high doses, as substitutes for prescribed medications, or in combination with multiple supplements. If you experience severe side effects, discontinue use immediately and seek medical attention.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Makes my oatmeal better](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R2BOJ2YCY5QAW3/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on March 31, 2023

Flavor Name: UnflavoredSize: 1.5 Pound (Pack of 1) [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






I tried a brand of oatmeal from the grocery store named for a type of brown bear, it is fortified with pea protein. It tasted nice and there was no crash, but it is also very expensive and contains more sugar than I'd like.



So I found this on Amazon, and just roll my own. I put a tablespoon in per serving. It is important to whisk the powder into the water thoroughly before it is added to the oatmeal, otherwise you'll have a bunch of not so great tasting lumps. Once blended properly and cooked in, I can for sure taste something a touch different than 'normal' oatmeal (the store bought stuff was the same) but it isn't unpleasant. One of my favorite breakfasts, you can a big pot to last several days (freezes well too!) with whatever fruit is in season.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Good quality, mixes well](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R6ML05C3M6VAD/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on July 1, 2023

Flavor Name: UnflavoredSize: 1.5 Pound (Pack of 1) [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






I like to add cocoa powder and stevia for a chocolate shake (sometimes olive oil too, especially with ice as it thickens it) and sometimes fiber. The taste is fine by itself too and nothing I have to gag down and it isn't lumpy or chalky. The only negative I have is the bag- I was never able to close it properly. I would buy again. It is cheaper but it is also a lot of powder for little protein so keep that in mind when evaluating price.

##### [_4.0 out of 5 stars_ Usually Great Organic Pea Protein](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1ZF1DK11XJIDQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on November 11, 2023

Flavor Name: UnflavoredSize: 1.5 Pound (Pack of 2) [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






I’ve got this a few times in the past and have been pleased with the taste, texture, and ability to fairly easily mix with water or milk. Unfortunately, the last batch seemed to really drop off in quality. I bought 2 of them, and both of them basically exploded with a plume of powder when opened. The powder getting everywhere also made it somewhat hard to close because the powder got in the grooves of the track that you use to close it, making it so that I had to fold over the flap and use a clip. I could’ve got past that and chalked it up to rough handling in transport, but then when I tried to mix it, the stuff basically foamed up into bubbles and was undrinkable (think of drinking shaving cream). Not only was the texture completely off, but I tried to drink the foam anyway, and it tasted a bit rancid.



Keep in mind that Amazon doesn’t allow returns on this, just like many other food items, so I basically just lost my money. I’m going to pour this into my compost pile outside, but it certainly isn’t fit for consumption. I really liked this product in the past as it’s hard to find organic pea protein, but I’m going to have to think twice before ordering from this supplier again.

_4.0 out of 5 stars_

##### Usually Great Organic Pea Protein










Reviewed in the United States on November 11, 2023







I’ve got this a few times in the past and have been pleased with the taste, texture, and ability to fairly easily mix with water or milk. Unfortunately, the last batch seemed to really drop off in quality. I bought 2 of them, and both of them basically exploded with a plume of powder when opened. The powder getting everywhere also made it somewhat hard to close because the powder got in the grooves of the track that you use to close it, making it so that I had to fold over the flap and use a clip. I could’ve got past that and chalked it up to rough handling in transport, but then when I tried to mix it, the stuff basically foamed up into bubbles and was undrinkable (think of drinking shaving cream). Not only was the texture completely off, but I tried to drink the foam anyway, and it tasted a bit rancid.



Keep in mind that Amazon doesn’t allow returns on this, just like many other food items, so I basically just lost my money. I’m going to pour this into my compost pile outside, but it certainly isn’t fit for consumption. I really liked this product in the past as it’s hard to find organic pea protein, but I’m going to have to think twice before ordering from this supplier again.

While it is an unflavoured product, it leaves an aftertaste in smoothies that I cannot explain. What's even more unusual is that it's fine in other foods, for example, pancakes or muffins. I bought this mostly to use in smoothies and ended up using it mostly for cooking and baking because of the aforementioned aftertaste and texture in smoothies. I liked it though, I just wouldn't call the texture "smooth".
